msg:We loved it so much we stayed another night!

Pros: 
- Great service 
- Stunning panoramic sea views 
- Beautiful beach
- Large rooms, comfy beds, large comfy bathrooms and slippers
- The segregated jacuzzi in the changing room area is so relaxing and having the option for swimming lessons is great
- Convenient and good location, close to shopping 
- Highly recommend the balcony room and a higher floor (2014 room was perfect!)
- The rooftop balcony in the horizon club room is great!

Could be better:
- The water bowl for the birds needs a thorough clean and fresh water.  A larger pen would be better for the rabbits health and longevity.
- The quality of the afternoon/dinner food served at the club room needs to improve, the range of beverages and quality of brand need to change to warrant the additional cost of paying for the club

FYI:
- If you‚Äôre returning to Beijing make sure to get a nucleic test within 48 hours! Beidaihe Hospital has a convenient testing station opposite the hospital - take passport! I had to return the next morning to get a print out as the app didn‚Äôt register our details.

Special mention:
- Thanks to Nick in level 1 Cafe during dinner for his attention to detail, he always ensured we had drinks and things were taken away in a timely manner. 
- Thanks so much to Jordan Wang for providing great service and helping us sort out our return to Beijing and to his female colleague! 
- Thanks to Oliver too for keeping everyone safe on the doors, we appreciated the efficient setup.
- Housekeeping service was prompt, helpful and cleaned very well.

msg:It was a great short trip. I take my kids to Beidaihe almost every year, mainly because it is close to home. It takes less than 2 hours to get there by high-speed rail. The kids won't feel tired or pressed for time on weekend trips. In previous years, I stayed in Liuzhuang. This time, in order to take my kids to experience a different Beidaihe, I chose the Shangri-La Hotel Qinhuangdao. Because it was my first time staying there, I didn't consider it very well and didn't choose a room with a balcony. I upgraded the room when I arrived at the hotel. It is recommended to choose a sea view room with a balcony, facing the sea... Spring is here. The room is very large, with an unobstructed view of the sea outside the window, and it is also very clean and comfortable. It takes only 2 minutes to go downstairs to the beach, and the kids can play with sand at any time and feed the seagulls with ham sausage. The sea water in mid-May is a little cold, and the temperature is not too high. I really need to bring a long-sleeved shirt these days. The child brought a long-sleeved shirt, and got it wet while playing with the sand. I went to Maoye Tiandi for dinner in the evening and bought one by the way. It is very necessary. It was raining this morning and the temperature was only about 10 degrees. I should be able to go to the sea to play during the summer vacation. The buffet at Qin Coffee on the first floor is also very good, and the children are very happy to eat. I would like to especially thank Jia Ting and Jiang Honglian at the front desk. The service was excellent, which made our stay very satisfactory and made our trip much more convenient.

Let me talk about the following three areas that need improvement:

3. The breakfast is a bit richer, and there is still a gap with the clubmed breakfast, I hope it can be improved.
Overall I am very satisfied with a happy trip, I will choose here next time.
